< review>
I've been wanting an undercut for about 2 years, but was reasonably nervous. I finally made the decision to do it, and after hunting around the valley for the right salon for me, I walked in Ascentia and immediately knew it was for me. The whole team is SO welcoming and I felt like a friend from the moment I walked in. Molly, who runs reception, is so friendly and helpful.

Today I finally got my long awaited cut, and it was such a good experience. Erica came in on her day off to help me out with her expertise and she did a phenomenal job on the cut, followed by Kayla fixing my HELLA messed up faded orange. Although we all agreed I need another appointment to be DONE, since we're going to buzz the undercut more and add some golden tones to my blonde once my hair has healed a bit, we were all SO happy with the result.

They listened to my thoughts and reservations, made me feel heard and comfortable, they were Covid-compliant, guided me on how to style my hair and aftercare as it heals from bleaching. Literally NEVER going back to fantastic sams again. Professional salons are where it's at. And this is the place to go!!!</review>

< Review>
A good place for pizza by Half-Moon bay and the boat docks. This is a small pizza shop that serves the Half-Moon Bay area. It is located on the corner of the road that runs onto the boat docks. The store has very limited parking and seating. We walked in and ordered a pizza. The staff was very friendly. We got it to go. It was done quickly and it was delicious. I recommend this for anyone wanting good pizza in the area.< /Review>

< review>
I have been to Sharp Mesa Vista inpatient  and outpatient programs and it is the best treatment I've received. You have to be you're own advocate and tell them what you need but once they know they help you. They treat you like an individual and respect your decision to either take medication or not.
They explained to me the options I had and didn't bother me that I chose to not take any prescriptions which I appreciated. I'm in cognitive group there outpatient now and it took two weeks to get used to it. They've helped me a lot. My therapist has found resources for me and my psychiatrist has helped with documents that I need for my medical leave claim. A psychiatric hospital is not exactly where anyone wants to be but sometimes you need it. It is hard to adjust and hard to be around others who have more extreme  symptoms than you do but it's worth it.

If you're reading this I hope you know that wherever you decide to seek treatment just know it's  okay to ask for help. No one's judging you as much as you judge yourself and I hope you get through this. It's difficult to be in a position in life where you're considering mental health treatment but it means you're willing to heal and that's awesome.</review>

< Text>
I was originally very happy with this place. They used to help me out a lot. Then one day I decided to get off of my opiate meds through a rehab clinic (Pacific Bay Recovery-- crooked and awful, do NOT go there) and that facility took me off of my mood stabilizer and anxiety medication. I asked to be put back on them at SMV but Dr. Moyer said "no" and laughed. I'm absolutely not privy to what's funny about that. I left as soon as possible and quickly found a new doctor. Turns out Dr. Moyer, who I'd been seeing for years, had misdiagnosed me. I'm Bipolar II, not simply depressed. I saw several other psychiatrists until I found my current one and they all diagnosed me with Bipolar II as well. I'm on Lamictal and Xanax XR among other things now and I'm much more functional than I've been in a very long time.

Also, on my first day during that visit post-rehab, Dr. Moyer was called to come see me as soon as possible because my symptoms were very bad. I cried a lot because I was terrified and didn't know why and the nurses told me that I'd have to deal with it until he came. I asked if they would give me a B-52 (a strong sedative for quickly calming patients) if I began acting violently but they said "we can't give you medication without your consent". Bulls**t. I was put on a 5150 once in a Sharp facility and they wasted no time restraining and sticking the guy across the hall, who had yelled and thrown a tray, with a B-52. They absolutely did not get his "consent" and nothing says they have to in those situations. Dr. Moyer eventually came near noon and gave me my basic medication which was nearly 24 hours overdue. The next day, however, he came extremely early. I asked him why he hadn't come early the day before when he was paged and he literally said "oh, I have to leave pretty soon so I came in early. I'm taking my kids on an Easter egg hunt." You're WHAT?! You ignored me yesterday when I had NO medication but today you come at 7am because you have to go appease kids you don't even have custody of?! (He's very openly divorced and depressed about it). I get that doctors need family time and sleep and all of those basic needs but he's dealing with mental health patients and that's not exactly something they care about. They care about relief and help in this trying time, not Easter egg hunts.

Another puzzling thing is they will let you read and use portable DVD players but they won't let you have portable video games because it will "distract from group meetings". And those other things don't? Also, I've been there enough times that I could definitely lead these meetings myself. You could go there for a one week stint and be able to do this. I'm not slow and neither are most of the patients there so we don't need to be talked down to. And if you don't go to the meetings you can be labeled as "non-compliant" and kept in the hospital longer.

Lastly, my friend Terry is dead. She died a couple of years ago, another victim of suicide. She was vibrant, fun, and very special to a lot of people. The nurses all knew she'd died but had to talk about it in hushed tones and tell me to say nothing. She was at SMV almost every time I was and she was always in the same condition with the same medications. Like me, I believe she was misdiagnosed which lead to her finally succeeding in a suicide attempt. She'd successfully pulled one off at a mental hospital (maybe SMV, maybe not since she never told me) but was revived after 10 minutes and was in a coma for two weeks. She was also likely the reason the doors are the way they are now because she hung herself there with her sheets but was found minutes before she successfully finished herself off. But she's dead now. And I at least partially blame SMV.</Text>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
My mother was recently released from the behavioral unit for seniors. She has multiple issues including anxiety, depression, early stages of dementia and an addiction to pain medicine. Dr. Khalafian is an exceptional psychiatrist! He is kind compassionate and very sensitive to the patient's needs yet he also understands the pharmacological agents that are necessary to bring the chemistry of the brain back into a more balanced approach. He called me at least twice to inform me on my mother's condition and prognosis.  He listened to my concerns as her son. He and the nursing staff were well on top of most of the issues that my mother faced, both physical and mental. They were very attentive to her needs and yet realistic to what they could achieve as goals. Also, my mother's social worker Tracy was a very efficient at setting up the necessary discharge contacts to ensure that my mother would receive further treatment. The issues of mental health are complex and difficult at times but Sharp Mesa Vista has done an exceptional job and continues to have a deep sense of commitment to its patients. My only concern is the limited number of beds available at a given time for such a large and growing need in our community.< /text>

<Review>Sharp Mesa Vista is an excellent facility for both detox and inpatient mental health services. They also have an excellent outpatient program too. I was reluctant to seek help for my issues because of punishing experiences at other facilities, particularly API in La Mesa, which is best avoided if your insurance provides alternatives. Mesa Vista is a comfortable, clean and spacious facility with top notch staff and excellent food. The staff consists of well educated professionals with advanced degrees. API by contrast, has a couple of doctors and nurses but, the day to day running of the facilities is done by certified "Mental Health Workers," which is probably a 600 hour certificate program. My only complaint with Sharp is this....While I was in detox, a social worker met with my girlfriend and advised her (more or less) to terminate our relationship. This is not something you do to somebody on his 3rd day in detox!!! She accepted his advice, returned to my room and broke the news to me at a time I was least able to cope with it. The end result is that I left detox early and continued with a relapse could very well have been fatal. Another thing worth mentioning is that recovery is a process, not an event. People in recovery often experience several failed attempts to get things right, which often entails multiple detox/hospitalization stays. Sharp seems to unofficially put a cap on the number of times you can utilize their facility, even if your insurance agrees to pay for your stay. I was in their outpatient and did very well, achieving multiple months of sobriety between relapses. Despite this, the last time I attempted to enroll in their outpatient program I was given the runaround big time. I always attended in the afternoons in the past, now they suggested I go at night, when it was least convenient. Then, when I reluctantly agreed to attend the night program at Mesa Vista, I was referred instead to their satellite program across town. Perhaps they didn't want me to bump into the unethical social worker who dispensed the near fatal advice. I hope you consider this to be a balanced and fair review.< /Review>< Pictures>

< Text>
I was hesitant to shop for an engagement ring online, but Yadav came through 100%! I worked w/Ellie initially via the chat function, who offered me a discount and helped to facilitate payment, which was super easy. In terms of the overall experience, I preferred picking up the phone and speaking with someone, as I felt the response time, information gathering and promised production deadlines via the chat/e-mail function post purchase were a little slow, which was frustrating and disappointing.

I was super fortunate that Susan answered the phone that day I called the store post purchase. She was AMAZING at helping me choose the right setting and with customizing it. She was super friendly, patient detailed orientated, professional and was always thinking two steps ahead. She always kept her word, whether that was to call/email me back or fill me in on something. The experience would not have been the same w/o Susan! She went above and beyond and so knowledgeable! She put my mind at ease.

Nan was also great in the payment process!

The turnaround time was great. Two weeks for custom made and shipping was super quick - 1 day FedEx and the box was nice and discreet!

The ring itself is GORGEOUS! The detail and high level quality is unmatched and I found the price for the diamond I got was a steal! Definitely would recommend YADAV to others!<//Text>

< Review>
I was so nervous about buying a diamond and creating a custom ring 100% on line (I live nowhere near CA). But all the local brick and mortar jewelry stores were just outrageous in the prices they quoted me.Â  The entire process,Â  start to finish could not have gone any smoother- I spoke primarily with Ellie and she was so patient and calm with all my dozens of questions. I purchased my center stone first but wanted to see it in person to confirm it was a keeper. Then they paid for me to ship it back to them and we started the custom design process.Â  I gave them a LOT of clear cut details and images to go on, but the end product is literally flawless and EXACTLY what I envisioned. Every detail from the right "tone" of rose gold, (I like more pink and less coppery) to the size of all the acccessory stones, to the "low profile" basket setting which was very important to me.Â  End result = 1.75 carat center oval stone (E color, VS1 clarity) set very low on a basket setting with a 1/2 pave band (2 mm wide) and a dainty hidden halo. Wedding band is 6 bezel set diamonds (0.5 carat total weight) on a 3mm rose gold band. Because the main ring is set so low, the wedding band cannot sit flush against it so they designed it in an "interrupted " fashion, meaning there is actually a gap in the wedding band to give it the illusion of sitting flush. I chose to solder the 2 rings together for this reason, so the wedding band would not spin and show the gap. It's like they read my mind and the best part is I expressed wanting it done in time for a trip to Turks and Caicos and they somehow managed to build this ring from scratch and have it in my hands in 7 days flat! It is stunning and I am so happy with it, 10/10 for Yadav!<//Review>

I bought my now fiance's engagement ring at the beginning of the year.

I found the Yadav site easy to use. The price was excellent. The service (mostly via email, plus one phone call) has been excellent as well.

After selecting the stone and ring combo, there was a notice on the site letting me know that it would take a few extra days since the stone had to be mounted. It took about 10 days to arrive, which seemed fairly quick to me.

I had to send the ring back to take it down a half a size. That process was pretty seamless and they paid for the shipping.

As far as the ring is concerned, my fiance LOVES it. She has received more compliments on it than I can count. I'm not much for jewelry myself, but I find myself staring at the stone. It's mesmerizing.

Overall, I think this purchase went as well as it could have. I don't regret not buying the ring locally. I got a great deal and there were no hiccups.

I 100% recommend this company.< /Review>

I am STUNNED by Yadav's service. <text>I ordered an engagement diamond through this company after seeing the one I liked on Rarecarat and had it shipped to me. Normally I make large purchases like this in person, especially if it was jewelry, so that I can inspect it and don't have to worry about shipping. Luckily, they had detailed descriptions, photos, and 360 video of the diamond itself so I felt confident enough to make the purchase.

Shipping was very very secure as the diamond was wonderfully packaged in its own little metal capsule, in a weighty box, inside shipping bag, inside a medium box, then AGAIN inside a large shipping box. It had multiple layers of protection and there was no way of telling it was a multi thousand dollar diamond inside. It also required signature on delivery.

The customer service was quick to respond if I wanted a refund, exchange, or shipping updates. The only downside was that the shipping took about two weeks.

Fiance absolutely loves the diamond and gets compliments on it all the time. Keep in mind this was a lab grown, 1,63, ideal cut, oval, vvs2, colorless, all for $4300. Robins Brothers wanted $10,000 for an equivalent lab grown diamond.

That is the last taboo, not related to this company. We were skeptical about getting a lab grown and the comments that may come along with it so we went to check out both lab grown and mined diamonds in person. The salesperson laid 3 lab grown and 3 mined in front of us to let us decide which one is which. After feeling confident on our choices we were completely wrong. There is no way to tell by eye the difference between lab grown and mined unless youre an absolute expert on it. So fellas, you can go up in size and quality by going this route.< /text>< pics>

</record></dataset><record>
<Text>Yadav is a honest and responsive business with good diamond and attitude but bad contractor for their rings. Me and my bf are planning to get engaged so I was looking for an engagement diamond online and found one that I like offered by Yadav. A bit on online diamonds: nowadays there's a ton of online diamond website, I think it's basically worth it to get diamonds online cuz the mark-up in physical shops are crazy, but since online diamond stores don't profit that much from their diamonds they may try to make that up by selling slightly over-priced settings. And even among online stores some are more expensive than others, like I think brilliant earth is more expensive than others; the same diamond may get listed on different store's website, like the one I picked was on Yadav and another online store called `with clarity', but Yadav's price is better, so I went with Yadav. Another funny thing is that although Yadav's diamond is cheaper than the other store, the setting is cheaper on the other store's website than Yadav's, so overall the market seems to be quite efficient. So I think the best strategy is to buy the diamond you like from the cheapest website online, and find a local physical jewelry shop to buy a setting. The mistake I made was buying a setting with Yadav: 1) it's expensive: $550 for 18k white gold solitaire setting 2) the first time they gave me a ring of the wrong size and wrong material (14 k instead of 18k) and 3) the second time they did ship me the ring size and material ring, but the diamond is clearly not set in the dead-center of the ring, and the 4 prongs of the ring were not equally spaced, so the ring looked very ugly. But they were super responsive and responsible during the whole process- they always reply email the next day, and they did stand up to what they promised - free return within 30 days with no question asked, and they gave me pre-paid shipping label with insurance on the shipping. I think what happened is that their business model is just to cut cost as much as possible so that they can earn money even when selling diamond at low margin, so they basically find the cheapest contractor out there to make their rings, which means their rings are poor-quality. So I would suggest buying diamond from them but not the ring, and find local jewelry shop to get a ring setting and set the diamond.< /Text><Rating>4</Rating><date>1565930738782</date><userid>100866558558407039137</userid>< username>

<user>106155413216713460647<//user><user_name>Beckett Horner<//user_name><Date>1548965340318</Date>< Rating>

< review>
The ring was beautiful and the diamond is great, but there is fire scale/discoloration on the ring after only 5 months. The ring was 18K yellow gold, and the soldered joints are turning a rose gold color. We confirmed with a local jeweler that the ring should not be turning this color; it should've been fused, not soldered. I expressed my disappointment with Yadav, and their response was that the discoloration was due to normal wear and tear (in 5 months!), and offered to polish the ring if we paid $70 to ship it back to them. I replied that the discoloration was not due to normal wear and tear but was in fact due to poor craftsmanship. That email was sent on November 16th, and I have not received a reply, hence this review.

UPDATE 1: I have head back from the owner; they agreed to pay to ship the ring back and check it out, so they have worked to rectify the situation. As such, I have adjusted my rating to 3 stars, and we'll see how the situation gets solved ultimately.

UPDATE 2: After back and forth, I was contacted by the owner, who agreed to pay to ship the ring back. Assumedly, they inspected the setting and determined the setting needed to be replaced. I believe they had a knew one built (although that was never made clear to me) and shipped it back. I believe the process took about 3 weeks.

We are satisfied with the service and my fiance gets compliments on the ring very often. I would recommend Yadav to a purchaser; if there are issues, they will fix them, you just have to stay on them.<//review>

<Gmap_id>0x808f7e2c76ec340f:0x828e09b5c38cbe2d<//Gmap_id><user_id>105906902151339330794< /user_id><response>None</response>< Review>
Yadav was recommended to me by a friend who likes to do meticulous research on things before buying them. I wasn't nervous about buying a diamond online necessarily, but I was unsure of how it would work, since the last time I bought a diamond, I went from store to store looking at loose diamonds until I found the right one.

I called Yadav and they assured me on the phone that they would overnight the diamond, and if it wasn't to my liking, I could just send it back, on their dime. What did I have to lose?

Yadav's website made it very easy to search through many different diamonds at once. You can enter in various search criteria in terms of cost, quality, etc., and then you can look at each actual diamond and its associated GIA report (if applicable). Most came with a full 360-view video, and I found this to be very easy to see any defect/inclusions at different angles.

Once I selected a diamond, it was overnighted to me, double-boxed in a standard large UPS priority box, with no obvious signage on the outside that the box contained anything of significant value. The return address did not even mention that it came from a jewelry store.

In my case, the diamond was exactly what was displayed online, down to every last detail. There were no unexpected surprises. What I saw was what I got, and it was stunning!

Fantastic quality at an amazing price. I am 100% satisfied, and would recommend Yadav to anyone looking for a diamond.</Review>
